<script id="wix-first-paint">
    if (window.ResizeObserver &&
        (!window.PerformanceObserver || !PerformanceObserver.supportedEntryTypes || PerformanceObserver.supportedEntryTypes.indexOf('paint') === -1)) {
        new ResizeObserver(function (entries, observer) {
            entries.some(function (entry) {
                var contentRect = entry.contentRect;
                if (contentRect.width > 0 && contentRect.height > 0) {
                    requestAnimationFrame(function (now) {
                        window.wixFirstPaint = now;
                        dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('wixFirstPaint'));
                    });
                    observer.disconnect();
                    return true;
                }
            });
        }).observe(document.body);
    }
</script>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:14px; margin-left:40px;"><span style="font-family:wfont_044ec0_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a84fc84d,wf_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a,orig_poppins_regular;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span style="font-size:14px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text">We recognize a special need to protect the personal information of children even over 13. How We Use Your Information</span></span></span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:14px; margin-left:80px;"><span style="font-family:wfont_044ec0_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a84fc84d,wf_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a,orig_poppins_regular;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span style="font-size:14px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text">We will primarily use information about you to provide the Services to you, such as, managing your information and accounts, answering requests for customer or technical support, etc. We will also use your information for administrative purposes, where we have a legal basis to do so, such as ensuring internal quality control and safety, authenticating and verifying individual identities, enhancing the operation of our Services, analyzing statistics relating to use of the Services, and improve our product and service offerings. We may use your information to provide you with updates related to the Services, in connection with our marketing and promotional efforts, to contact you regarding administrative notices, to tailor and provide you with content and advertisements via email campaigns, targeted on-line advertisements on social media and at trade shows and other events. For any questions regarding our marketing practices, or if you would like to withdraw consent of the use of your information for such purposes, please contact us in the Contact Us section below. We may use information in connection with any beta testing you participate in and to resolve disputes, troubleshoot problems and enforce our agreements with you, including but not limited to our Terms of Service. Finally, we may use your information for other purposes as requested by you or as permitted by applicable law, such as to promote safety, integrity and security of our Services, to offer tools for sharing content with friends and to comply with our legal obligations, including if we have good-faith belief it is necessary.</span></span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:14px; line-height:0.8em; margin-left:80px;"><span style="font-family:wfont_044ec0_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a84fc84d,wf_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a,orig_poppins_regular;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span style="font-size:14px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span class="wixGuard wixui-rich-text__text">​</span></span></span></p>

We may use third-party Application Program Interfaces (“APIs”) and software development kits (“SDKs”) as part of the functionality of our Services.</span></span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:14px; line-height:0.5em; margin-left:40px;"><span style="font-family:wfont_044ec0_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a84fc84d,wf_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a,orig_poppins_regular;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span style="font-size:14px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span class="wixGuard wixui-rich-text__text">​</span></span></span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:14px; line-height:0.5em; margin-left:40px;"><span style="font-family:wfont_044ec0_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a84fc84d,wf_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a,orig_poppins_regular;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span style="font-size:14px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span class="wixGuard wixui-rich-text__text">​</span></span></span></p>

Your Privacy Rights</span></span></span></h1>

<h1 class="font_0 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:14px; margin-left:40px;"><span style="font-family:wfont_044ec0_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a84fc84d,wf_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a,orig_poppins_regular;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span style="font-size:14px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text">We believe that you should have the ability to access and edit the personal information we have collected about you, and we encourage you to promptly update your personal information if it changes. </li>
<li class="wixui-rich-text__text">
<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:14px;"><span style="font-family:wfont_044ec0_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a84fc84d,wf_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a,orig_poppins_regular;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span style="font-size:14px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text">not be discriminated against for exercising the right to know or right to request deletion;</span></span></p>

To fulfill your request, we will need to verify your identity. Only you, or someone legally authorized to act on your behalf, may make a request related to personal information collected about you. <p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:14px; line-height:0.5em;"><span style="font-family:wfont_044ec0_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a84fc84d,wf_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a,orig_poppins_regular;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span style="font-size:14px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span class="wixGuard wixui-rich-text__text">​</span></span></span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:14px; margin-left:40px;"><span style="font-family:wfont_044ec0_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a84fc84d,wf_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a,orig_poppins_regular;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span style="font-size:14px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text">We take steps to ensure that your information is treated securely and in accordance with this Privacy Policy. <p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:14px; line-height:1.4em; margin-left:40px;"><span style="font-family:wfont_044ec0_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a84fc84d,wf_8a940bae2f2740e789023089a,orig_poppins_regular;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><span style="font-size:14px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text">By using our Services or by providing personal information to us, you agree that we may communicate with you electronically regarding security, privacy, and administrative issues relating to your use of our Services.</span></span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">“Sales” of Personal Information under the CCPA</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">​</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">For purposes of the CCPA, Argarium does not “sell” personal information, nor do we have actual knowledge of any “sale” of personal information of minors under 16 years of age.</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">Additional Privacy Rights for California Residents</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">If you are a California resident, subject to certain exceptions and applicable law, you may have certain rights in relation to information we process about you</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">​</p>

<ul class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">
<li class="wixui-rich-text__text">
<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">Right to Know.&nbsp;In relation to your right to access described above, you may request that we disclose to you the categories and specific pieces of personal information that we have collected about you in the preceding 12 months, the categories of sources from which your personal information is collected, the business or commercial purpose for collecting your personal information, the categories of personal information that we disclosed for a business purpose in the preceding 12 months, the categories of third parties with whom we have shared your personal information, and the business or commercial purpose for each disclosure.</p>
</li>
<li class="wixui-rich-text__text">
<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">Right to Delete.&nbsp;In relation to your right to delete as described above, you may request that we delete any personal information that we have collected from you.</p>
</li>
<li class="wixui-rich-text__text">
<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">Non-Discrimination.&nbsp;You have the right not to receive discriminatory treatment by us for the exercise of their rights conferred by the CCPA.</p>
</li>
<li class="wixui-rich-text__text">
<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">Authorized Agent.&nbsp;Only you, or someone legally authorized to act on your behalf, may make a verifiable consumer request related to your personal information. You may also make a verifiable consumer request on behalf of your minor child. To designate an authorized agent, please contact us at the addresses in the Contact Us section below.</p>
</li>
<li class="wixui-rich-text__text">
<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">Verification.&nbsp;To protect your privacy, we will take the following steps to verify your identity before fulfilling your request. When you make a request, we will ask you to provide sufficient information that allows us to reasonably verify you are the person about whom we collected personal information or an authorized representative, which may include your name, email address, or Game Platform User ID.</p>
</li>
</ul>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">​</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">If you are a California resident and would like to exercise any of your rights under the CCPA, please contact us at the addresses in the Contact Us section below. We will process such requests in accordance with applicable laws.</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">​</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">Accessibility.&nbsp;This Privacy Policy uses industry-standard technologies and was developed in line with the World Wide Web Consortium’s Web Content Accessibility Guidelines, version 2.1. If you wish to print this policy, please do so from your web browser or by saving the page as a PDF.</p>

<h1 class="font_0 wixui-rich-text__text">&nbsp; 8. Disclosures to Users Outside the United States</h1>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text">&nbsp;As we are an Israeli company, it may be necessary to transfer your personal information to Israel [and to the U.S. and other third countries outside of the UK/EEA in order for us to provide the Services to you and such third countries may have data protection laws that are different and less protective from the laws where you live. Where we transfer UK/EEA personal data to third parties in third countries, we utilize Standard Contractual Clauses approved by the European Commission, and rely on the European Commission’s adequacy decisions about certain countries, as applicable, for such transfers.</p>
